  (: is-variable 
    (-> Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (is-variable $x) 
    (== 
      (get-metatype $x) Variable))
  :- dynamic'is-variable'/1.

  'is-variable'(_x1) :-
    eval([==, ['get-metatype', _x1], 'Variable'], _x1).
  (: lazy-or 
    (-> Bool Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (lazy-or False $x) $x)
  :- dynamic'lazy-or'/2.

  'lazy-or'(A, _x2) :-
    eval_false(A).

    eval_false(A).


  (= 
    (lazy-or True $x) True)
  :- dynamic'lazy-or'/2.

  'lazy-or'(A, _x3) :-
    eval_true(A),
    _x3='True'.
  (: is-expression 
    (-> Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (is-expression $x) 
    (== 
      (get-metatype $x) Expression))
  :- dynamic'is-expression'/1.

  'is-expression'(_x4) :-
    eval([==, ['get-metatype', _x4], 'Expression'], _x4).
  (: is-closed 
    (-> Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (is-closed $x) 
    (if 
      (is-variable $x) False 
      (if 
        (== () $x) True 
        (if 
          (is-expression $x) 
          (and 
            (let $head 
              (car-atom $x) 
              (is-closed $head)) 
            (let $tail 
              (cdr-atom $x) 
              (is-closed $tail))) True))))
  :- dynamic'is-closed'/1.

  'is-closed'(_x5) :-
    (   eval_true(['is-variable', _x5])
    *-> _x5='False'
    ;   (   eval_true([==, [], _x5])
        *-> A='True'
        ;   (   eval_true(['is-expression', _x5])
            *-> ( eval(['car-atom', _x5], _head1),
                  'is-closed'(_head1, B),
                  eval(['cdr-atom', _x5], _tail1)
                ),
                'is-closed'(_tail1, B),
                B=C
            ;   C='True'
            ),
            C=A
        ),
        A=_x5
    ).
'is-closed'(_x5) :-
    (   eval_true(['is-variable', _x5])
    *-> A='False',
        A=_x5
    ;   (   eval_true([==, [], _x5])
        *-> B='True',
            B=C

                D=E
            ;   F='True',
                F=E
            ),
            E=C
        ),
        C=_x5
